3b3(rgyud): la rnam par rtsen pa'i dbang du gyur pa/gzungs rab tu thob pa/spobs pa zad pa med pa/nyon mongs pa rnams spangs pa/nye ba'i kun nas nyin mongs
3b4(rgyud): pa rnams nye bar zhi bar gyur pa/ring por mi thogs par rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa mngon par 'grub par 'gyur ba/bdud kyi dpung rab tu 'joms
3b5(rgyud): pachos kyi rnga shin tu brdung ba/mu stegs can du ma btul nas/yongasu dga' ba'i bsam pa bskyed pa la 'god pa/chos kyi 'khor lo dam
3b6(rgyud): pa yongasu bskor nas/lha dang mi rnams sgrol bar byed pa/phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams rab tu rgyun pa/'gro ba drug pa'i sems can dag
3b7(rgyud): la phan dogs pa/ye shes chen po yongasu rdzogs pa/bzod pa chen pa phun sum tshogs pa/byams pa dang /snying rje chen po'i sems la rab tu
4a1(rgyud): gnas pa/shin tu brtan pa'i stobs chen po dang ldan pa//sangs rgyas mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa/yongasu mya ngan las mi 'da'

4a3(rgyud): dus gsum gyi chos rnams las mi skye ba'i bzod pa rtogs par gyur pa/theg pa gnyis po dag gi spyod yul las yang dag par 'das pa/thabs mokhas pa
4a4(rgyud): chen pos 'jig rten pa rnams 'dul bar byed pa/ston pa chen po'i bstan pa rnams yang dag par sgrogs pa/gsang ba'i chos dang shin tu zab pa'i stong pa nyid
4a5(rgyud): rtogs shing khong du chud pas/the tshomo dang som nyi med par gyur pa sha stag la/'di lta ste/byang chub sems dpa' thogs pa med par chos kyi 'khor lo
4a6(rgyud): bskor ba dang /byang chub sems dpa' rtag par chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar sems bskyod pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' rtag par brtson pa dang /byang
4a7(rgyud): chub sems dpa' rgyun mi 'chad pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' byams pa dang /byang chub sems dpa'i 'jam dpal dang /byang chub sems dpa' spyan
4b1(rgyud): ras gzigs dbang phyug dang /byang chub sems dpa' gzungs la rang dbang du gyur pa'i rgyal po dang /byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa chen po bgrod pa'i rgyal po dang /
4b2(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa'i re rab mchog gri rgyal po dang /byang chub sems dpa' shin tu thob pa'i rgya mtsho'i rgyal po dang /byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'o tog drang /
4b3(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i tog chen po dang /byang chub sems dpa' sa'i snying po dang /byang chub sems dpa' na mkho'i snying po dang /byang chub sems dpa' rin
4b4(rgyud): po che gri dbang phyug dang /byang chub sems dpa' log ni rdo rje dang /byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba'i stobs dang /byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi stobs chen dang /
4b5(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' bkod pa'i 'od chen dang /byang chub sems dpa' gsor 'od bkod pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' rnamo dge tshul khrims dang /byang chub sems dpa'
4b6(rgyud): rtag tu mnyam par gzhag pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' blo gros shin tu rnam dag dang /byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus brtan pa dang /byang chub sems dpa'
4b7(rgyud): na mkha' dang mtshungs pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' smon lam chen po mo gcod pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' sman stong dang /byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i
5a1(rgyud): nad rnam par sel ba dang /byang chub sems dpa' sman pa'i rgyal po dang /byang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa dga' ba'i rgyal po dang /byang chub sems
5a2(rgyud): dpa' lung bstan mchog thob dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen rnam dag 'od zer dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen chos 'dzin dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin
5a3(rgyud): chen grags pa'i dga' ba dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen grags pa mtha' yas ston dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin tshon seng ge'i nga ro dang
5a4(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen glang po che'i rgyal po'i nga ro dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen bkyonas dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen yon tan dang /
5a5(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen nyi ma'i snying po dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen zla ba'i snying po dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen skar ma'i 'od dang /byung
5a6(rgyud): chub sems dpa' sprin chen mo'i 'od dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen glog 'od dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen 'brug dbyangs dang /byang chub sems
5a7(rgyud): dpa' sprin chen shes rab kyi char gyis kun tu khyab pa dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen po rnam dag char rgyal dang /byang chub se mos dpa' sprin chen me tog
5b1(rgyud): ljoldan shing rgyal ba dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen pad+ma sngon po'i gsung dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen rlon pa che'i can dan gyi dris lus bsil bar byed pa dang /byung
5b2(rgyud): chub sems dpa' sprin tshon mun sel dang /byang chub sems dpa' sprin che ni rab rab 'joms la sogs pa/'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs chen po tshang med pa de dag
5b3(rgyud): kyang so so nas phyi dro'i dus kyi tshe/ting nge 'dzin las langs nas/bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logasu dong ste/bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag byas nas/g.yas
5b4(rgyud): phyogs su bskor ba byas te/phyogs gcig tu 'khod par gyur to//bzhin yang li tsa byi gzhan nu l-I 'bum phrag brgya stong du ma 'dus par gyur pa la 'od lto ste/gzhan nu
5b5(rgyud): seng ge'i 'od dang /gzhon nu seng ge'i blo gros dang /gzhon nu chos kyi byin dang /gzhon nu dbang pos byi ni dang /gzhon nu 'od chen dang /gzhin dpal che ni dang /gnon nu sang+yas skyong dang /gzhin

7b3(rgyud): kyi tshe/ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs nas/'khor gyi dkyil 'khor la rnam par gzigs nas/tshig su bcad de bka' stsal pa/gser 'od dam pa gya nom tshos//mad

8a1(rgyud): po ma tshad dang //tshe zad dang ni tshe nyams dang //sdig pa'i mtshan ma mngon snang dang //lha rnams kyis ni spangs pa dang //gnyen gshen kun gyis sngang/
8a2(rgyud): ba dang //'khor rnams dang ni 'bral ba dang //phan tshun mi mthun rtsod pa dang //gza' skar mi rungs gnod byas shing //byed ste ma log pas zin pa dang //mya ngan mang
8a3(rgyud): pos nyon mongs shing //sdug bsngal mang pos gzir ba dang //rmi lam ltas ngan mthong ba'i rgyus//mya ngan dag ni skyed gyur na//de yis khrus ni rab 'byor la//gos gca

8a5(rgyud): mdo sde 'di yi byin rlabs mthus//ye 'brog mang po mi byed cing //gzhan yang sdug bsngal sna tshogs bgegs//thams cad ma lus sel bar byed//'jig rten skyong dang
8a6(rgyud): rgyal chen bzhi//blon po chen po 'khor rnams dang //gnod sbyin mang po tshad med rnams//rtse gcig sems kyis skyob par byed//spobs pa che bo'i lha mo dang //nai rony+dza nar
8a7(rgyud): gnas pa'i lha//lha mo 'phrog ma 'byung mo'i ma//sras brtan so yi lha mo dang //tshangs pa dbang po brgya byin dang //klu yi rgyal po mi 'am ci//gser 'dab bya yi rgyal po/

8b3(rgyud): ste 'dri zos naso//gzhan la rgya cher ston po dang //gal te sems kyis yi rang dang //mchod pa bshams nas mchod byed na//de 'dra'i gang zag de dag ni//bskal pa

9a6(rgyud): snyam du rgya gang dang /rkyen gang gi phyir de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa sku tshe thung ste/lo brgyad cur gyur snyamo//gzhan yang 'dri snyam du bcom ldan 'das kyis

9b2(rgyud): skyed du sems can gyi srog ma bcad cing /dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam spyad pa dang /rtag par bza' ba dang /btung ba dog bkres pa'i sems can thams cad la

9b7(rgyud): sna bzhi las mngon par grub pa/lha'i rin po che'i gos kyis ge yogs pa dang /gzhan yang gdan de la pad+ma dam pa rin po che sna tshogs kyis rgyan pa/tshad de bzhin

10a5(rgyud): tu khyab par mdzad de/lha'i me tog gi char yang mngon par phob lha'i rol mo'i sil snyan rnams kyang dkrol bar gyur te/de'i tshe 'dzam bu'i gling 'di dang /stong gsum gyi

10b2(rgyud): bshungs pa dag ni gzhan gyis bkur bar gyur/dri ma dang bcas pa dag ni lus gtsang bar gyur te/'jig rten gyi khams 'dir phan 'dogs pa'i dngos po ngo mtshar rmad du

10b5(rgyud): bltas nas/gzhan yang 'di snyam du de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan yang sku tshe'i tshad 'ba' zhig la the tsom gyi sems skyes par gyur na//

11a1(rgyud): pa'i 'jig rten na tshangs pa dang /bdud dang /dge sbyong dang /bram ze dang /mi dang mi ma yin pa gang gis kyang /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku

12b1(rgyud): pa dang /klog pa dang /kha ton du 'don pa dang /kun chub par byas nas gzhan dag la yang dag par bstan pa dang /skur pa 'debs par mi 'gyur bar mdzad par bzhed pa'i phyir/

12b3(rgyud): 'da' ba mthong bar gyur na/gus pas rim gro yang mi byed/shin tu phrad par dka' ba'i 'du shes kyang mi bskyed la/de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i mdo sde zab mo dag

12b6(rgyud): na/nor rdzas dag la ngo mtshar dang mthong bar dka' ba'i 'du shes skye bar mi 'gyur ro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/pha'i nor rdzas dag la rtag pa'i 'du shes pa'i phyir ro//rigs kyi bu sems
12b7(rgyud): can mang po de dag kyang /de bzhin du gal te/de bzhin gshegs po yongasu mya ngan las mi 'da' ba mthong bar gyur na/ngo mtshar dang mthong bar dka' ba'i 'du shes skye bar mi
13a1(rgyud): 'gyur ro//de ci'i phyir zhe na/rtag par mthong ba'i phyir ro//rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/mi zhig phye ma dbul zhing nor rdzas kyis phongs pa

13a3(rgyud): gyur na/ngo mtshar dang phrad par dka' ba'i 'du shes bskyed nas/de'i tshe mi dbul po de nor rdzas yongs su gnyer ba'i phyir ro//sbyor ba'i thabs rgya cher bshams nas/le lo//

17b4(rgyud): rim bzhin bshad par bya//sangs rgyas spyod yul bsam dka' bas//'jig rten dag na mtshungs med pa//chos sku ngo bo nyid bzhugs pas//rnal 'byor sgrom la khyad par med//
17b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas sku kun mtshungs pas na//chos gsungs pa yang de bzhin te//sangs rgyas rnams la mdzad mi mnga'//bzod ma nyid nas skye ba med//bcom ldan rdo rje'i sku yin yang //

17b7(rgyud): sems can+da rnams la phan gdags phyir//thabs kyis sku gdung bzhug pa yin//chos sku yang dag sangs rgyas pas//ches dbyings de bzhin gshegs pa yin//yang dag

40b1(rgyud): can gang zhig ngan 'gro gnas gyur nas//mi chen rab 'bar lus kun khyab pa dag/rnga sgra dam pa 'di ni thos gyur nas//sdug bsngal bral nas sangs rgyas skyabs 'gro/
